{\footnotesize\ttfamily adi\+\_\+port\+\_\+config\+\_\+e\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+port\+\_\+get\+\_\+config (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



General A\+DI Use Functions ~\newline
 

These functions allow for interaction with any A\+DI port type ~\newline
 Gets the configuration for the given A\+DI port.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports.

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_adebbf89bed5c3464bd77712c4c53edef}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_adebbf89bed5c3464bd77712c4c53edef}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!adi\_analog\_calibrate@{adi\_analog\_calibrate}}
\index{adi\_analog\_calibrate@{adi\_analog\_calibrate}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{adi\_analog\_calibrate()}{adi\_analog\_calibrate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+calibrate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calibrates the analog sensor on the specified port and returns the new calibration value. 

This method assumes that the true sensor value is not actively changing at this time and computes an average from approximately 500 samples, 1 ms apart, for a 0.\+5 s period of calibration. The average value thus calculated is returned and stored for later calls to the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a34a3205b4beecc2efb561a068ac869e7}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a0a62ec5516d617b8282f9f1c21e68e15}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated\+\_\+\+H\+R()}} functions. These functions will return the difference between this value and the current sensor value when called.

Do not use this function when the sensor value might be unstable (gyro rotation, accelerometer movement).

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The A\+DI port to calibrate (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{})\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The average sensor value computed by this function 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_aaec9c097a2fb6ae1632954591eea35d7}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_aaec9c097a2fb6ae1632954591eea35d7}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!adi\_analog\_read@{adi\_analog\_read}}
\index{adi\_analog\_read@{adi\_analog\_read}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{adi\_analog\_read()}{adi\_analog\_read()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the 12-\/bit value of the specified port. 

The value returned is undefined if the analog pin has been switched to a different mode.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an analog input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The A\+DI port (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) for which the value will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The analog sensor value, where a value of 0 reflects an input voltage of nearly 0 V and a value of 4095 reflects an input voltage of nearly 5 V 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a34a3205b4beecc2efb561a068ac869e7}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a34a3205b4beecc2efb561a068ac869e7}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated@{adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated}}
\index{adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated@{adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated()}{adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the 12 bit calibrated value of an analog input port. 

The \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_adebbf89bed5c3464bd77712c4c53edef}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+calibrate()}} function must be run first. This function is inappropriate for sensor values intended for integration, as round-\/off error can accumulate causing drift over time. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a0a62ec5516d617b8282f9f1c21e68e15}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated\+\_\+\+H\+R()}} instead.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an analog input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The A\+DI port (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) for which the value will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The difference of the sensor value from its calibrated default from -\/4095 to 4095 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a0a62ec5516d617b8282f9f1c21e68e15}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a0a62ec5516d617b8282f9f1c21e68e15}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR@{adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR}}
\index{adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR@{adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR()}{adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated\+\_\+\+HR (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the 16 bit calibrated value of an analog input port. 

The \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_adebbf89bed5c3464bd77712c4c53edef}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+calibrate()}} function must be run first. This is intended for integrated sensor values such as gyros and accelerometers to reduce drift due to round-\/off, and should not be used on a sensor such as a line tracker or potentiometer.

The value returned actually has 16 bits of \char`\"{}precision\char`\"{}, even though the A\+DC only reads 12 bits, so that error induced by the average value being between two values when integrated over time is trivial. Think of the value as the true value times 16.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an analog input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The A\+DI port (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) for which the value will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The difference of the sensor value from its calibrated default from -\/16384 to 16384 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a4acc4110678a3f4ae8f6b793b2dc1793}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a4acc4110678a3f4ae8f6b793b2dc1793}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!adi\_digital\_read@{adi\_digital\_read}}
\index{adi\_digital\_read@{adi\_digital\_read}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{adi\_digital\_read()}{adi\_digital\_read()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+digital\+\_\+read (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the digital value (1 or 0) of a port configured as a digital input. 

If the port is configured as some other mode, the digital value which reflects the current state of the port is returned, which may or may not differ from the currently set value. The return value is undefined for ports configured as any mode other than a Digital Input.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a digital input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The A\+DI port to read (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{})\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
True if the pin is H\+I\+GH, or false if it is L\+OW 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_af67d01f4e0aad2806c699e249d869977}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_af67d01f4e0aad2806c699e249d869977}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press@{adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press}}
\index{adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press@{adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press()}{adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+digital\+\_\+get\+\_\+new\+\_\+press (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets a rising-\/edge case for a digital button press. 

This function is not thread-\/safe. Multiple tasks polling a single button may return different results under the same circumstances, so only one task should call this function for any given button. E.\+g., \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Task}{Task}} A calls this function for buttons 1 and 2. \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Task}{Task}} B may call this function for button 3, but should not for buttons 1 or 2. A typical use-\/case for this function is to call inside opcontrol to detect new button presses, and not in any other tasks.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a digital input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The A\+DI port to read (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{})\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the button is pressed and had not been pressed the last time this function was called, 0 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_adbbe71d4934bbe5218b33405207f5f39}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_adbbe71d4934bbe5218b33405207f5f39}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+motor\+\_\+stop (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Stops the motor on the given port. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an motor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The A\+DI port to set (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{})\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+encoder\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_adc7331a863ca648693c688af1ae9a940}{adi\+\_\+encoder\+\_\+t}}}]{enc }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the number of ticks recorded by the encoder. 

There are 360 ticks in one revolution.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an encoder

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The signed and cumulative number of counts since the last start or reset 
\end{DoxyReturn}

This should be in port 1, 3, 5, or 7 (\textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}C\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}E\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}G\textquotesingle{}). \\
\hline
{\em port\+\_\+bottom} & The \char`\"{}bottom\char`\"{} wire from the encoder sensor \\
\hline
{\em reverse} & If \char`\"{}true\char`\"{}, the sensor will count in the opposite direction\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An adi\+\_\+encoder\+\_\+t object to be stored and used for later calls to encoder functions 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Sets the encoder value to zero. 

It is safe to use this method while an encoder is enabled. It is not necessary to call this method before stopping or starting an encoder.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an encoder

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno.

\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!adi\_ultrasonic\_get@{adi\_ultrasonic\_get}}
\index{adi\_ultrasonic\_get@{adi\_ultrasonic\_get}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{adi\_ultrasonic\_get()}{adi\_ultrasonic\_get()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a642e06a44cad02177d4111261e17c3df}{adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+t}}}]{ult }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the current ultrasonic sensor value in centimeters. 

If no object was found, zero is returned. If the ultrasonic sensor was never started, the return value is undefined. Round and fluffy objects can cause inaccurate values to be returned.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an ultrasonic


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ult} & The adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+t object from \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a2bd844aa49e221c1e68c0b94d148c3b4}{adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+init()}} to read\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The distance to the nearest object in m$^\wedge$-\/4 (10000 indicates 1 meter), measured from the sensor\textquotesingle{}s mounting points. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a2bd844aa49e221c1e68c0b94d148c3b4}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a2bd844aa49e221c1e68c0b94d148c3b4}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!adi\_ultrasonic\_init@{adi\_ultrasonic\_init}}

\hline

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a7ee7cf11c1a604af68b9373f4b7c8799}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a7ee7cf11c1a604af68b9373f4b7c8799}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!adi\_gyro\_get@{adi\_gyro\_get}}
\index{adi\_gyro\_get@{adi\_gyro\_get}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{adi\_gyro\_get()}{adi\_gyro\_get()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily double pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a9c451728d4193f1a4e59d7dc489ac292}{adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t}}}]{gyro }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the current gyro angle in tenths of a degree. 

Unless a multiplier is applied to the gyro, the return value will be a whole number representing the number of degrees of rotation times 10.

There are 360 degrees in a circle, thus the gyro will return 3600 for one whole rotation.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a gyro


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em gyro} & The adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t object for which the angle will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The gyro angle in degrees. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a6ee6e73d3be33d0b2f5c4bfbe37f2d4c}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a6ee6e73d3be33d0b2f5c4bfbe37f2d4c}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!adi\_gyro\_init@{adi\_gyro\_init}}
\index{adi\_gyro\_init@{adi\_gyro\_init}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{adi\_gyro\_init()}{adi\_gyro\_init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a9c451728d4193f1a4e59d7dc489ac292}{adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t}} pros\+::c\+::adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{double}]{multiplier }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initializes a gyroscope on the given port. 

If the given port has not previously been configured as a gyro, then this function starts a 1300 ms calibration period.

It is highly recommended that this function be called from \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8h_a9efe22aaead3a5e936b5df459de02eba}{initialize()}} when the robot is stationary to ensure proper calibration.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of A\+DI Ports E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a gyro


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The A\+DI port to initialize as a gyro (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) \\
\hline
{\em multiplier} & A scalar value that will be multiplied by the gyro heading value supplied by the A\+DI\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t object containing the given port, or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the initialization failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a79a193e42f59415cf1f860812a7248d6}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a79a193e42f59415cf1f860812a7248d6}}

Resets the gyroscope value to zero.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void pros\+::c\+::task\+\_\+notify\+\_\+when\+\_\+deleting (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a1d7e0825b8d8876e8cd8ece3f9115293}{task\+\_\+t}}}]{target\+\_\+task,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a1d7e0825b8d8876e8cd8ece3f9115293}{task\+\_\+t}}}]{task\+\_\+to\+\_\+notify,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a42ea99b5e5d38da0b98154609cf6c570}{notify\+\_\+action\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{notify\+\_\+action }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Notify a task when a target task is being deleted. 

This function will configure the P\+R\+OS kernel to call task\+\_\+notify\+\_\+ext(task\+\_\+to\+\_\+notify, value, action, N\+U\+L\+L) when target\+\_\+task is deleted.

\end{DoxyParams}

Creates a recursive mutex which can be locked recursively by the owner.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool pros\+::c\+::sem\+\_\+wait (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_abc53a59ab4c3c8f2d7660e63990be7a7}{sem\+\_\+t}}}]{sem,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{timeout }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Waits for the semaphore\textquotesingle{}s value to be greater than 0. 

If the value is already greater than 0, this function immediately returns.

See \href{https://pros.cs.purdue.edu/v5/tutorials/multitasking.html\#semaphores}{\texttt{ https\+://pros.\+cs.\+purdue.\+edu/v5/tutorials/multitasking.\+html\#semaphores}} for details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em sem} & Semaphore to wait on \\
\hline
{\em timeout} & Time to wait before the semaphore\textquotesingle{}s becomes available. A timeout of 0 can be used to poll the sempahore. T\+I\+M\+E\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+M\+AX can be used to block indefinitely.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
True if the semaphore was successfully take, false otherwise. If false is returned, then errno is set with a hint about why the sempahore couldn\textquotesingle{}t be taken. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a1224c0d9b29e68b15971b90d2fdb6f98}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a1224c0d9b29e68b15971b90d2fdb6f98}}

\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{distance\_get\_confidence()}{distance\_get\_confidence()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::distance\+\_\+get\+\_\+confidence (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the confidence in the distance reading. 

This is a value that has a range of 0 to 63. 63 means high confidence, lower values imply less confidence. Confidence is only available when distance is $>$ 200mm (the value 10 is returned in this scenario).

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Distance}{Distance}} Sensor

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ac7ce5918ef247fbfbebadb8b87417ced}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ac7ce5918ef247fbfbebadb8b87417ced}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate@{ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate}}
\index{ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate@{ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate()}{ext\_adi\_analog\_calibrate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+calibrate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calibrates the analog sensor on the specified port and returns the new calibration value. 

This method assumes that the true sensor value is not actively changing at this time and computes an average from approximately 500 samples, 1 ms apart, for a 0.\+5 s period of calibration. The average value thus calculated is returned and stored for later calls to the \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a34a3205b4beecc2efb561a068ac869e7}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a0a62ec5516d617b8282f9f1c21e68e15}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated\+\_\+\+H\+R()}} functions. These functions will return the difference between this value and the current sensor value when called.

Do not use this function when the sensor value might be unstable (gyro rotation, accelerometer movement).

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port to calibrate (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{})\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The average sensor value computed by this function 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ad23c527e73c2008d5bf49030efa255ef}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ad23c527e73c2008d5bf49030efa255ef}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_analog\_read@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read}}
\index{ext\_adi\_analog\_read@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_analog\_read()}{ext\_adi\_analog\_read()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the 12-\/bit value of the specified port. 

The value returned is undefined if the analog pin has been switched to a different mode.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an analog input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) for which the value will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

The analog sensor value, where a value of 0 reflects an input voltage of nearly 0 V and a value of 4095 reflects an input voltage of nearly 5 V 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a2dd9e7a9e761ed80088bcf7f44920a42}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a2dd9e7a9e761ed80088bcf7f44920a42}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated}}
\index{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated()}{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the 12 bit calibrated value of an analog input port. 

The \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_adebbf89bed5c3464bd77712c4c53edef}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+calibrate()}} function must be run first. This function is inappropriate for sensor values intended for integration, as round-\/off error can accumulate causing drift over time. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a0a62ec5516d617b8282f9f1c21e68e15}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated\+\_\+\+H\+R()}} instead.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an analog input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) for which the value will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The difference of the sensor value from its calibrated default from -\/4095 to 4095 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a4e1d85f2e166adf83743b9fde5c504e8}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a4e1d85f2e166adf83743b9fde5c504e8}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR}}
\index{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR@{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR()}{ext\_adi\_analog\_read\_calibrated\_HR()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+read\+\_\+calibrated\+\_\+\+HR (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the 16 bit calibrated value of an analog input port. 

The \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_adebbf89bed5c3464bd77712c4c53edef}{adi\+\_\+analog\+\_\+calibrate()}} function must be run first. This is intended for integrated sensor values such as gyros and accelerometers to reduce drift due to round-\/off, and should not be used on a sensor such as a line tracker or potentiometer.

The value returned actually has 16 bits of \char`\"{}precision\char`\"{}, even though the A\+DC only reads 12 bits, so that error induced by the average value being between two values when integrated over time is trivial. Think of the value as the true value times 16.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an analog input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) for which the value will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The difference of the sensor value from its calibrated default from -\/16384 to 16384 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ad030dfc04f9d5adb0861f940472974f0}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ad030dfc04f9d5adb0861f940472974f0}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_digital\_read@{ext\_adi\_digital\_read}}
\index{ext\_adi\_digital\_read@{ext\_adi\_digital\_read}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_digital\_read()}{ext\_adi\_digital\_read()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+digital\+\_\+read (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the digital value (1 or 0) of a port configured as a digital input. 

If the port is configured as some other mode, the digital value which reflects the current state of the port is returned, which may or may not differ from the currently set value. The return value is undefined for ports configured as any mode other than a Digital Input.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a digital input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port to read (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{})\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
True if the pin is H\+I\+GH, or false if it is L\+OW 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ac5b25457c1f1277dd545b6fab326299c}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ac5b25457c1f1277dd545b6fab326299c}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press@{ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press}}
\index{ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press@{ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press()}{ext\_adi\_digital\_get\_new\_press()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+digital\+\_\+get\+\_\+new\+\_\+press (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets a rising-\/edge case for a digital button press. 

This function is not thread-\/safe. Multiple tasks polling a single button may return different results under the same circumstances, so only one task should call this function for any given button. E.\+g., \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Task}{Task}} A calls this function for buttons 1 and 2. \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Task}{Task}} B may call this function for button 3, but should not for buttons 1 or 2. A typical use-\/case for this function is to call inside opcontrol to detect new button presses, and not in any other tasks.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a digital input


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port to read (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{})\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the button is pressed and had not been pressed the last time this function was called, 0 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a638e7d47bbdde4b545be396d4cb20eea}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a638e7d47bbdde4b545be396d4cb20eea}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a628d2ba74a77b5d590e4b865e3f4a7aa}{ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+t}}}]{ult }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the current ultrasonic sensor value in centimeters. 

If no object was found, zero is returned. If the ultrasonic sensor was never started, the return value is undefined. Round and fluffy objects can cause inaccurate values to be returned.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). \hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The distance to the nearest object in m$^\wedge$-\/4 (10000 indicates 1 meter), measured from the sensor\textquotesingle{}s mounting points. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_ultrasonic\_init()}{ext\_adi\_ultrasonic\_init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a628d2ba74a77b5d590e4b865e3f4a7aa}{ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+t}} pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port\+\_\+ping,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port\+\_\+echo }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates an ultrasonic object and configures the specified ports accordingly. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an ultrasonic


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port\+\_\+ping} & The port connected to the orange O\+U\+T\+P\+UT cable. This should be in port 1, 3, 5, or 7 (\textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}C\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}E\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}G\textquotesingle{}). \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port\+\_\+echo} & The port connected to the yellow I\+N\+P\+UT cable. This should be in the next highest port following port\+\_\+ping.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+t object to be stored and used for later calls to ultrasonic functions 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Disables the ultrasonic sensor and voids the configuration on its ports. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as an ultrasonic


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ult} & The adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+t object from \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a2bd844aa49e221c1e68c0b94d148c3b4}{adi\+\_\+ultrasonic\+\_\+init()}} to stop\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a0d75771553832ae16e7b45833fb095fd}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a0d75771553832ae16e7b45833fb095fd}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_gyro\_get@{ext\_adi\_gyro\_get}}
\index{ext\_adi\_gyro\_get@{ext\_adi\_gyro\_get}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_gyro\_get()}{ext\_adi\_gyro\_get()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily double pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+get (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_aeb1fda9da4589cd3cd2e9efe5693f308}{ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t}}}]{gyro }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the current gyro angle in tenths of a degree. 

Unless a multiplier is applied to the gyro, the return value will be a whole number representing the number of degrees of rotation times 10.

There are 360 degrees in a circle, thus the gyro will return 3600 for one whole rotation.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a gyro


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em gyro} & The adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t object for which the angle will be returned\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The gyro angle in degrees. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a62cddb9a1858256f0fa03effc89ddb20}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a62cddb9a1858256f0fa03effc89ddb20}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!ext\_adi\_gyro\_init@{ext\_adi\_gyro\_init}}
\index{ext\_adi\_gyro\_init@{ext\_adi\_gyro\_init}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ext\_adi\_gyro\_init()}{ext\_adi\_gyro\_init()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_aeb1fda9da4589cd3cd2e9efe5693f308}{ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t}} pros\+::c\+::ext\+\_\+adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{smart\+\_\+port,  }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{adi\+\_\+port,  }\item[{double}]{multiplier }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initializes a gyroscope on the given port. 

If the given port has not previously been configured as a gyro, then this function starts a 1300 ms calibration period.

It is highly recommended that this function be called from \mbox{\hyperlink{main_8h_a9efe22aaead3a5e936b5df459de02eba}{initialize()}} when the robot is stationary to ensure proper calibration.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ Either the A\+DI port value or the smart port value is not within its valid range (A\+DI port\+: 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, or \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}; smart port\+: 1-\/21). E\+A\+D\+D\+R\+I\+N\+U\+SE -\/ The port is not configured as a gyro


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em smart\+\_\+port} & The smart port number that the A\+DI Expander is in \\
\hline
{\em adi\+\_\+port} & The A\+DI port to initialize as a gyro (from 1-\/8, \textquotesingle{}a\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}A\textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}H\textquotesingle{}) \\
\hline
{\em multiplier} & A scalar value that will be multiplied by the gyro heading value supplied by the A\+DI\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An adi\+\_\+gyro\+\_\+t object containing the given port, or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the initialization failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a91d5a238cdf4fcde887bbb88e3a7ecb0}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a91d5a238cdf4fcde887bbb88e3a7ecb0}}

Calibrate I\+MU. 

This takes approximately 2 seconds, and is a non-\/blocking operation.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an Inertial Sensor E\+A\+G\+A\+IN -\/ The sensor is already calibrating

\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a73029aa0aa910f9b740ffe6def05e830}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a73029aa0aa910f9b740ffe6def05e830}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!imu\_set\_data\_rate@{imu\_set\_data\_rate}}
\index{imu\_set\_data\_rate@{imu\_set\_data\_rate}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{imu\_set\_data\_rate()}{imu\_set\_data\_rate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::imu\+\_\+set\+\_\+data\+\_\+rate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{rate }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the Inertial Sensor\textquotesingle{}s refresh interval in milliseconds. 

The rate may be specified in increments of 5ms, and will be rounded down to the nearest increment. The minimum allowable refresh rate is 5ms. The default rate is 10ms.

As values are copied into the shared memory buffer only at 10ms intervals, setting this value to less than 10ms does not mean that you can poll the sensor\textquotesingle{}s values any faster. However, it will guarantee that the data is as recent as possible.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an Inertial Sensor E\+A\+G\+A\+IN -\/ The sensor is still calibrating


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 Inertial Sensor port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em rate} & The data refresh interval in milliseconds \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_aa44bc46059f8aca47f3317320f1cd5bc}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_aa44bc46059f8aca47f3317320f1cd5bc}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily double pros\+::c\+::imu\+\_\+get\+\_\+rotation (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the total number of degrees the Inertial Sensor has spun about the z-\/axis. 

This value is theoretically unbounded. Clockwise rotations are represented with positive degree values, while counterclockwise rotations are represented with negative ones.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an Inertial Sensor E\+A\+G\+A\+IN -\/ The sensor is still calibrating


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 Inertial Sensor port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The degree value or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+F if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Get the Inertial Sensor\textquotesingle{}s heading relative to the initial direction of its x-\/axis. 

This value is bounded by (-\/360,360). Clockwise rotations are represented with positive degree values, while counterclockwise rotations are represented with negative ones.

\index{lcd\_shutdown@{lcd\_shutdown}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lcd\_shutdown()}{lcd\_shutdown()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool pros\+::c\+::lcd\+\_\+shutdown (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Turns off the Legacy L\+CD Emulator. 

Calling this function will clear the entire display, and you will not be able to call any further L\+L\+E\+MU functions until another call to lcd\+\_\+initialize.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The L\+CD has not been initialized. Call \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a36a50f90e2186a37abce6cf36d5df6a3}{lcd\+\_\+initialize()}} first.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
True if the operation was successful, or false otherwise, setting errno values as specified above. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_adb97914cdf57d801b60962f9be046c8f}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_adb97914cdf57d801b60962f9be046c8f}}

\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!lcd\_read\_buttons@{lcd\_read\_buttons}}
\index{lcd\_read\_buttons@{lcd\_read\_buttons}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lcd\_read\_buttons()}{lcd\_read\_buttons()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint8\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::lcd\+\_\+read\+\_\+buttons (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the button status from the emulated three-\/button L\+CD. 

The value returned is a 3-\/bit integer where 1 0 0 indicates the left button is pressed, 0 1 0 indicates the center button is pressed, and 0 0 1 indicates the right button is pressed. 0 is returned if no buttons are currently being pressed.

Note that this function is provided for legacy A\+PI compatibility purposes, with the caveat that the V5 touch screen does not actually support pressing multiple points on the screen at the same time.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The buttons pressed as a bit mask 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_aeb04d3a78a7596b89366603a0068763b}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_aeb04d3a78a7596b89366603a0068763b}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a1a381afe1cabb7c9b5dd5a734a5ee4a3}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a1a381afe1cabb7c9b5dd5a734a5ee4a3}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{controller\_is\_connected()}{controller\_is\_connected()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::controller\+\_\+is\+\_\+connected (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_af1323f00203099060d46f722b1fbd460}{controller\+\_\+id\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Checks if the controller is connected. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ A value other than E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+T\+ER or E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+N\+ER is given. E\+A\+C\+C\+ES -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the controller port.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em id} & The ID of the controller (e.\+g. the master or partner controller). Must be one of C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+T\+ER or C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+N\+ER\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the controller is connected, 0 otherwise 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a1a7c4e6bcb39260bf7ce5b1a58638753}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a1a7c4e6bcb39260bf7ce5b1a58638753}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!controller\_get\_analog@{controller\_get\_analog}}
\index{controller\_get\_analog@{controller\_get\_analog}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{controller\_get\_analog()}{controller\_get\_analog()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::controller\+\_\+get\+\_\+analog (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_af1323f00203099060d46f722b1fbd460}{controller\+\_\+id\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{id,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a8bdd0963e2bc0d4fbe03435eee8a5ca5}{controller\+\_\+analog\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{channel }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the value of an analog channel (joystick) on a controller. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ A value other than E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+T\+ER or E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+N\+ER is given. E\+A\+C\+C\+ES -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the controller port.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em id} & The ID of the controller (e.\+g. the master or partner controller). Must be one of C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+T\+ER or C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+N\+ER \\
\hline
{\em channel} & The analog channel to get. Must be one of A\+N\+A\+L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+L\+E\+F\+T\+\_\+X, A\+N\+A\+L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+L\+E\+F\+T\+\_\+Y, A\+N\+A\+L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+R\+I\+G\+H\+T\+\_\+X, A\+N\+A\+L\+O\+G\+\_\+\+R\+I\+G\+H\+T\+\_\+Y\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The current reading of the analog channel\+: \mbox{[}-\/127, 127\mbox{]}. If the controller was not connected, then 0 is returned 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::controller\+\_\+get\+\_\+battery\+\_\+capacity (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_af1323f00203099060d46f722b1fbd460}{controller\+\_\+id\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{id }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the battery capacity of the given controller. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ A value other than E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+T\+ER or E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+N\+ER is given. E\+A\+C\+C\+ES -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the controller port.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em id} & The ID of the controller (e.\+g. the master or partner controller). Must be one of E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+T\+ER or E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+N\+ER\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The controller\textquotesingle{}s battery capacity 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::controller\+\_\+get\+\_\+digital (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_af1323f00203099060d46f722b1fbd460}{controller\+\_\+id\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{id,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a8c380ff02828ee53954bc0ce274253ed}{controller\+\_\+digital\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{button }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Checks if a digital channel (button) on the controller is currently pressed. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ A value other than E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+T\+ER or E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+N\+ER is given. E\+A\+C\+C\+ES -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the controller port.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em id} & The ID of the controller (e.\+g. the master or partner controller). Must be one of C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+T\+ER or C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+N\+ER \\
\hline
{\em button} & The button to read. Must be one of D\+I\+G\+I\+T\+A\+L\+\_\+\{R\+I\+G\+HT,D\+O\+WN,L\+E\+FT,UP,A,B,Y,X,R1,R2,L1,L2\}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the button on the controller is pressed. If the controller was not connected, then 0 is returned 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ac98088451005003975c19dda4e20a1f8}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ac98088451005003975c19dda4e20a1f8}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!controller\_get\_digital\_new\_press@{controller\_get\_digital\_new\_press}}
\index{controller\_get\_digital\_new\_press@{controller\_get\_digital\_new\_press}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{controller\_get\_digital\_new\_press()}{controller\_get\_digital\_new\_press()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::controller\+\_\+get\+\_\+digital\+\_\+new\+\_\+press (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_af1323f00203099060d46f722b1fbd460}{controller\+\_\+id\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{id,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a8c380ff02828ee53954bc0ce274253ed}{controller\+\_\+digital\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{button }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns a rising-\/edge case for a controller button press. 

This function is not thread-\/safe. Multiple tasks polling a single button may return different results under the same circumstances, so only one task should call this function for any given button. E.\+g., \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Task}{Task}} A calls this function for buttons 1 and 2. \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Task}{Task}} B may call this function for button 3, but should not for buttons 1 or 2. A typical use-\/case for this function is to call inside opcontrol to detect new button presses, and not in any other tasks.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ A value other than E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+T\+ER or E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+N\+ER is given. E\+A\+C\+C\+ES -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the controller port.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em id} & The ID of the controller (e.\+g. the master or partner controller). Must be one of C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+S\+T\+ER or C\+O\+N\+T\+R\+O\+L\+L\+E\+R\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+N\+ER \\
\hline
{\em button} & The button to read. Must be one of D\+I\+G\+I\+T\+A\+L\+\_\+\{R\+I\+G\+HT,D\+O\+WN,L\+E\+FT,UP,A,B,Y,X,R1,R2,L1,L2\}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the button on the controller is pressed and had not been pressed the last time this function was called, 0 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a7bdcfd084f96b7eda87867de947997b8}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a7bdcfd084f96b7eda87867de947997b8}}

E\+A\+C\+C\+ES -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the controller port.

\hline

\end{DoxyNote}

\hline
{\em rumble\+\_\+pattern} & A string consisting of the characters \textquotesingle{}.\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}-\/\textquotesingle{}, and \textquotesingle{} \textquotesingle{}, where dots are short rumbles, dashes are long rumbles, and spaces are pauses. {\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::rotation\+\_\+set\+\_\+reversed (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{bool}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Set the \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor\textquotesingle{}s direction reversed flag. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as an \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em value} & Determines if the direction of the \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Rotation}{Rotation}} Sensor is reversed or not.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if operation succeeded or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!task\_create@{task\_create}}
\index{task\_create@{task\_create}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{task\_create()}{task\_create()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a1d7e0825b8d8876e8cd8ece3f9115293}{task\+\_\+t}} pros\+::c\+::task\+\_\+create (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_aece0aa29b1f1538115228d2197239f98}{task\+\_\+fn\+\_\+t}}}]{function,  }\item[{void $\ast$const}]{parameters,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{prio,  }\item[{const uint16\+\_\+t}]{stack\+\_\+depth,  }\item[{const char $\ast$const}]{name }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a new task and add it to the list of tasks that are ready to run. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+O\+M\+EM -\/ The stack cannot be used as the T\+CB was not created.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em function} & Pointer to the task entry function \\
\hline
{\em parameters} & Pointer to memory that will be used as a parameter for the task being created. This memory should not typically come from stack, but rather from dynamically (i.\+e., malloc\textquotesingle{}d) or statically allocated memory. \\
\hline
{\em prio} & The priority at which the task should run. T\+A\+S\+K\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+O\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+A\+U\+LT plus/minus 1 or 2 is typically used. \\
\hline
{\em stack\+\_\+depth} & The number of words (i.\+e. 4 $\ast$ stack\+\_\+depth) available on the task\textquotesingle{}s stack. T\+A\+S\+K\+\_\+\+S\+T\+A\+C\+K\+\_\+\+D\+E\+P\+T\+H\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+A\+U\+LT is typically sufficienct. \\
\hline
{\em name} & A descriptive name for the task. This is mainly used to facilitate debugging. The name may be up to 32 characters long.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A handle by which the newly created task can be referenced. If an error occurred, N\+U\+LL will be returned and errno can be checked for hints as to why task\+\_\+create failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a9f5bd026f982b738d8761c443af586da}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a9f5bd026f982b738d8761c443af586da}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!task\_delete@{task\_delete}}
\index{task\_delete@{task\_delete}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{task\_delete()}{task\_delete()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void pros\+::c\+::task\+\_\+delete (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a1d7e0825b8d8876e8cd8ece3f9115293}{task\+\_\+t}}}]{task }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Removes a task from the R\+T\+OS real time kernel\textquotesingle{}s management. 

The task being deleted will be removed from all ready, blocked, suspended and event lists.

Memory dynamically allocated by the task is not automatically freed, and should be freed before the task is deleted.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em task} & The handle of the task to be deleted. Passing N\+U\+LL will cause the calling task to be deleted. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a4954a1ed8e37fd9b758ff98bf3ecf7d4}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a4954a1ed8e37fd9b758ff98bf3ecf7d4}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!task\_delay@{task\_delay}}
\index{task\_delay@{task\_delay}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{task\_delay()}{task\_delay()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void pros\+::c\+::task\+\_\+delay (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{milliseconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Delays a task for a given number of milliseconds. 

This is not the best method to have a task execute code at predefined intervals, as the delay time is measured from when the delay is requested. To delay cyclically, use \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_a151eaf730a10d101bff15013a76b9aa8}{task\+\_\+delay\+\_\+until()}}.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em milliseconds} & The number of milliseconds to wait (1000 milliseconds per second) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a6a62f5325d65f95436762552df547d73}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a6a62f5325d65f95436762552df547d73}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!delay@{delay}}
\index{delay@{delay}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{delay()}{delay()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void pros\+::c\+::delay (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{milliseconds }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a151eaf730a10d101bff15013a76b9aa8}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a151eaf730a10d101bff15013a76b9aa8}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!task\_delay\_until@{task\_delay\_until}}
\index{task\_delay\_until@{task\_delay\_until}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{task\_delay\_until()}{task\_delay\_until()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void pros\+::c\+::task\+\_\+delay\+\_\+until (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint32\+\_\+t $\ast$const}]{prev\+\_\+time,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{delta }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Delays a task until a specified time. 

This function can be used by periodic tasks to ensure a constant execution frequency.

The task will be woken up at the time $\ast$prev\+\_\+time + delta, and $\ast$prev\+\_\+time will be updated to reflect the time at which the task will unblock.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em prev\+\_\+time} & A pointer to the location storing the setpoint time. This should typically be initialized to the return value of \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_1_1c_aa247cd38039665b7ac4b0d0920b83c80}{millis()}}. \\
\hline
{\em delta} & The number of milliseconds to wait (1000 milliseconds per second) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ab49c228af50a4677d45e4622fb5f982b}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ab49c228af50a4677d45e4622fb5f982b}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::task\+\_\+get\+\_\+count (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gets the number of tasks the kernel is currently managing, including all ready, blocked, or suspended tasks. 

A task that has been deleted, but not yet reaped by the idle task will also be included in the count. Tasks recently created may take one context switch to be counted.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The number of tasks that are currently being managed by the kernel. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::task\+\_\+notify (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a1d7e0825b8d8876e8cd8ece3f9115293}{task\+\_\+t}}}]{task }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sends a simple notification to task and increments the notification counter. 

See \href{https://pros.cs.purdue.edu/v5/tutorials/topical/notifications.html}{\texttt{ https\+://pros.\+cs.\+purdue.\+edu/v5/tutorials/topical/notifications.\+html}} for details.

\end{DoxyParams}

Always returns true. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_af21b3326026e04f277e85236f4ff503a}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_af21b3326026e04f277e85236f4ff503a}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!task\_notify\_ext@{task\_notify\_ext}}
\index{task\_notify\_ext@{task\_notify\_ext}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{task\_notify\_ext()}{task\_notify\_ext()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::task\+\_\+notify\+\_\+ext (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a1d7e0825b8d8876e8cd8ece3f9115293}{task\+\_\+t}}}]{task,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{value,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a42ea99b5e5d38da0b98154609cf6c570}{notify\+\_\+action\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}}}]{action,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{prev\+\_\+value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sends a notification to a task, optionally performing some action. 

Will also retrieve the value of the notification in the target task before modifying the notification value.

See \href{https://pros.cs.purdue.edu/v5/tutorials/topical/notifications.html}{\texttt{ https\+://pros.\+cs.\+purdue.\+edu/v5/tutorials/topical/notifications.\+html}} for details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em task} & The task to notify \\
\hline
{\em value} & The value used in performing the action \\
\hline
{\em action} & An action to optionally perform on the receiving task\textquotesingle{}s notification value \\
\hline
{\em prev\+\_\+value} & A pointer to store the previous value of the target task\textquotesingle{}s notification, may be N\+U\+LL\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Dependent on the notification action. For N\+O\+T\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+A\+C\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+W\+R\+I\+TE\+: return 0 if the value could be written without needing to overwrite, 1 otherwise. For all other N\+O\+T\+I\+F\+Y\+\_\+\+A\+C\+T\+I\+ON values\+: always return 0 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a15f1230bbc0fe029caf775a393b4a897}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a15f1230bbc0fe029caf775a393b4a897}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!task\_notify\_take@{task\_notify\_take}}
\index{task\_notify\_take@{task\_notify\_take}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{task\_notify\_take()}{task\_notify\_take()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::task\+\_\+notify\+\_\+take (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{bool}]{clear\+\_\+on\+\_\+exit,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{timeout }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Waits for a notification to be nonzero. 

See \href{https://pros.cs.purdue.edu/v5/tutorials/topical/notifications.html}{\texttt{ https\+://pros.\+cs.\+purdue.\+edu/v5/tutorials/topical/notifications.\+html}} for details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em clear\+\_\+on\+\_\+exit} & If true (1), then the notification value is cleared. If false (0), then the notification value is decremented. \\
\hline
{\em timeout} & Specifies the amount of time to be spent waiting for a notification to occur.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The value of the task\textquotesingle{}s notification value before it is decremented or cleared 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{mutex\_take@{mutex\_take}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mutex\_take()}{mutex\_take()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool pros\+::c\+::mutex\+\_\+take (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_ab15ea84d90257d70b44e8e04519864d2}{mutex\+\_\+t}}}]{mutex,  }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{timeout }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Takes and locks a mutex, waiting for up to a certain number of milliseconds before timing out. 

See \href{https://pros.cs.purdue.edu/v5/tutorials/topical/multitasking.html\#mutexes}{\texttt{ https\+://pros.\+cs.\+purdue.\+edu/v5/tutorials/topical/multitasking.\+html\#mutexes}} for details.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mutex} & \mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Mutex}{Mutex}} to attempt to lock. \\
\hline
{\em timeout} & Time to wait before the mutex becomes available. A timeout of 0 can be used to poll the mutex. T\+I\+M\+E\+O\+U\+T\+\_\+\+M\+AX can be used to block indefinitely.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
True if the mutex was successfully taken, false otherwise. If false is returned, then errno is set with a hint about why the the mutex couldn\textquotesingle{}t be taken. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a7f20ed94cee8e04d491743b4b34feda1}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a7f20ed94cee8e04d491743b4b34feda1}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::serial\+\_\+enable (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



\mbox{\hyperlink{classpros_1_1Serial}{Serial}} communication functions ~\newline
 

These functions allow programmers to communicate using U\+A\+RT over R\+S485 ~\newline
 Enables generic serial on the given port.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function must be called before any of the generic serial functions will work.
\end{DoxyNote}
This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+A\+C\+C\+ES -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the port.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a764ae0c3adf9c45564fdfa6ac398968e}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a764ae0c3adf9c45564fdfa6ac398968e}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a01af0f44a069891e14e17953cd3a6260}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a01af0f44a069891e14e17953cd3a6260}} 
\index{pros::c@{pros::c}!serial\_flush@{serial\_flush}}
\index{serial\_flush@{serial\_flush}!pros::c@{pros::c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{serial\_flush()}{serial\_flush()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::serial\+\_\+flush (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Clears the internal input and output F\+I\+FO buffers. 

This can be useful to reset state and remove old, potentially unneeded data from the input F\+I\+FO buffer or to cancel sending any data in the output F\+I\+FO buffer.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function does not cause the data in the output buffer to be written, it simply clears the internal buffers. Unlike stdout, generic serial does not use buffered IO (the F\+I\+FO buffers are written as soon as possible).
\end{DoxyNote}
This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+A\+C\+C\+ES -\/ Another resource is currently trying to access the port.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vision\_create\_color\_code()}{vision\_create\_color\_code()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_a71f2011a47e95558bb534b05c16c7f2b}{vision\+\_\+color\+\_\+code\+\_\+t}} pros\+::c\+::vision\+\_\+create\+\_\+color\+\_\+code (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{sig\+\_\+id1,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{sig\+\_\+id2,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{sig\+\_\+id3,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{sig\+\_\+id4,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{sig\+\_\+id5 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a color code that represents a combination of the given signature I\+Ds. 

If fewer than 5 signatures are to be a part of the color code, pass 0 for the additional function parameters.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+I\+N\+V\+AL -\/ Fewer than two signatures have been provided or one of the signatures is out of its \mbox{[}1-\/7\mbox{]} range (or 0 when omitted).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
{\em sig\+\_\+id1} & The first signature id \mbox{[}1-\/7\mbox{]} to add to the color code \\
\hline
{\em sig\+\_\+id2} & The second signature id \mbox{[}1-\/7\mbox{]} to add to the color code \\
\hline
{\em sig\+\_\+id3} & The third signature id \mbox{[}1-\/7\mbox{]} to add to the color code \\
\hline
{\em sig\+\_\+id4} & The fourth signature id \mbox{[}1-\/7\mbox{]} to add to the color code \\
\hline
{\em sig\+\_\+id5} & The fifth signature id \mbox{[}1-\/7\mbox{]} to add to the color code\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A vision\+\_\+color\+\_\+code\+\_\+t object containing the color code information. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_ad0b47d5910ba2a6e5d52629f2b93c3e6}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_ad0b47d5910ba2a6e5d52629f2b93c3e6}}

Gets the nth largest object according to size\+\_\+id. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a vision sensor E\+D\+OM -\/ size\+\_\+id is greater than the number of available objects. E\+H\+O\+S\+T\+D\+O\+WN -\/ Reading the vision sensor failed for an unknown reason.

{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The vision\+\_\+object\+\_\+s\+\_\+t object corresponding to the given size id, or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if an error occurred. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vision\_read\_by\_size()}{vision\_read\_by\_size()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::vision\+\_\+read\+\_\+by\+\_\+size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{size\+\_\+id,  }\item[{const uint32\+\_\+t}]{object\+\_\+count,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepros_ae619120558539c13e53b5a6f42fb4375}{vision\+\_\+object\+\_\+s\+\_\+t}} $\ast$const}]{object\+\_\+arr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Reads up to object\+\_\+count object descriptors into object\+\_\+arr. 

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21), or fewer than object\+\_\+count number of objects were found. E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a vision sensor E\+D\+OM -\/ size\+\_\+id is greater than the number of available objects.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline
 & {\em size\+\_\+id} & The object to read from a list roughly ordered by object size (0 is the largest item, 1 is the second largest, etc.) \\
\hline
 & {\em object\+\_\+count} & The number of objects to read \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em object\+\_\+arr} & A pointer to copy the objects into\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The number of object signatures copied. This number will be less than object\+\_\+count if there are fewer objects detected by the vision sensor. Returns P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the port was invalid, an error occurred, or fewer objects than size\+\_\+id were found. All objects in object\+\_\+arr that were not found are given V\+I\+S\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+O\+B\+J\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+\_\+\+S\+IG as their signature. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacepros_1_1c_a0f38715b935eae0421d59e5102d98155}\label{namespacepros_1_1c_a0f38715b935eae0421d59e5102d98155}}

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a vision sensor

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{vision\_set\_zero\_point()}{vision\_set\_zero\_point()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int32\+\_\+t pros\+::c\+::vision\+\_\+set\+\_\+zero\+\_\+point (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{port,  }\item[{vision\+\_\+zero\+\_\+e\+\_\+t}]{zero\+\_\+point }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sets the (0,0) coordinate for the Field of View. 

This will affect the coordinates returned for each request for a vision\+\_\+object\+\_\+s\+\_\+t from the sensor, so it is recommended that this function only be used to configure the sensor at the beginning of its use.

This function uses the following values of errno when an error state is reached\+: E\+N\+X\+IO -\/ The given value is not within the range of V5 ports (1-\/21). E\+N\+O\+D\+EV -\/ The port cannot be configured as a vision sensor


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em port} & The V5 port number from 1-\/21 \\
\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

1 if the operation was successful or P\+R\+O\+S\+\_\+\+E\+RR if the operation failed, setting errno. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
